```dart
->

  Future<void> refundKey() async {
    if (keys < 5) {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      setState(() {
        keys++;
      });
      await prefs.setInt('keys', keys);
      print('Key refunded! Current keys: $keys'); // ë””ë²„ê·¸ìš©
    }
  }
```

## 2. 24ì‹œê°„ ì¶©ì „ ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ + ë‚¨ì€ ì‹œê°„ í‘œì‹œ

```dart
class _HomeScreenState extends State<HomeScreen> {
  int keys = 5; // ì—´ì‡  ê°œìˆ˜
  
  @override

    loadKeys();

->

class _HomeScreenState extends State<HomeScreen> {
  int keys = 5; // ì—´ì‡  ê°œìˆ˜
  Timer? _timer;
  String timeUntilNextKey = '';
  
  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    loadKeys();
    checkKeyRecharge();
    _startTimer();
  }
  
  @override
  void dispose() {
    _timer?.cancel();
    super.dispose();
  }
```

```dart
  Future<void> checkKeyRecharge() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final lastKeyTime = prefs.getInt('last_key_time') ?? 0;
    final now = DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
    final timeDiff = now - lastKeyTime;
    
    // 12ì‹œê°„ = 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000 = 43,200,000 ë°€ë¦¬ì´ˆ
    const keyRechargeTime = 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    
    if (keys < 5 && timeDiff >= keyRechargeTime) {
      final keysToAdd = (timeDiff ~/ keyRechargeTime).clamp(0, 5 - keys);
      setState(() {
        keys = (keys + keysToAdd).clamp(0, 5);
      });
      await saveKeys();
    }
  }

->

  Future<void> checkKeyRecharge() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final lastKeyTime = prefs.getInt('last_key_time') ?? 0;
    final now = DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
    final timeDiff = now - lastKeyTime;
    
    // 24ì‹œê°„ = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 = 86,400,000 ë°€ë¦¬ì´ˆ
    const keyRechargeTime = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    
    if (keys < 5 && timeDiff >= keyRechargeTime) {
      final keysToAdd = (timeDiff ~/ keyRechargeTime).clamp(0, 5 - keys);
      setState(() {
        keys = (keys + keysToAdd).clamp(0, 5);
      });
      await saveKeys();
    }
    
    _updateTimeUntilNextKey();
  }
  
  void _startTimer() {
    _timer = Timer.periodic(const Duration(seconds: 1), (timer) {
      _updateTimeUntilNextKey();
    });
  }
  
  Future<void> _updateTimeUntilNextKey() async {
    if (keys >= 5) {
      setState(() {
        timeUntilNextKey = '';
      });
      return;
    }
    
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final lastKeyTime = prefs.getInt('last_key_time') ?? DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
    final now = DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
    const keyRechargeTime = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24ì‹œê°„
    
    final nextKeyTime = lastKeyTime + keyRechargeTime;
    final timeLeft = nextKeyTime - now;
    
    if (timeLeft <= 0) {
      await checkKeyRecharge();
    } else {
      final hours = (timeLeft ~/ (1000 * 60 * 60));
      final minutes = ((timeLeft % (1000 * 60 * 60)) ~/ (1000 * 60));
      final seconds = ((timeLeft % (1000 * 60)) ~/ 1000);
      
      setState(() {
        timeUntilNextKey = '${hours.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}:${minutes.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}:${seconds.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}';
      });
    }
  }
```

```dart
                const SizedBox(height: 20),
```

## 3. 3í•­ ì—°ì‚° ë¬¸ì œ ìˆ˜ì • (9, 10ë²ˆì§¸ë§Œ + í•œìë¦¿ìˆ˜)

QuizScreenì˜ 3í•­ ì—°ì‚° ë¡œì§ì„ ìˆ˜ì •í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

```dart
  void generateQuestion() {
    if (currentQuestion >= 9) {
      // 9-10ë²ˆì§¸ ë¬¸ì œëŠ” 3í•­ í˜¼í•© ë¬¸ì œ
      _generateThreeTermQuestion();
    } else {
      // 1-8ë²ˆì§¸ ë¬¸ì œëŠ” 2í•­ ë¬¸ì œ
      _generateTwoTermQuestion();
    }
    
    _answerController.clear();
    isAnswered = false;
    isCorrect = false;
  }

->

  void generateQuestion() {
    if (currentQuestion == 9 || currentQuestion == 10) {
      // 9, 10ë²ˆì§¸ ë¬¸ì œë§Œ 3í•­ í˜¼í•© ë¬¸ì œ
      _generateThreeTermQuestion();
    } else {
      // 1-8ë²ˆì§¸ ë¬¸ì œëŠ” 2í•­ ë¬¸ì œ
      _generateTwoTermQuestion();
    }
    
    _answerController.clear();
    isAnswered = false;
    isCorrect = false;
  }
```

```dart
  void _generateThreeTermQuestion() {
    final random = Random();
    isThreeTermQuestion = true;
    
    // ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ì™€ ë‘ ë²ˆì§¸ ì—°ì‚° ì„ íƒ
    final operations = ['+', '-'];
    operation = operations[random.nextInt(operations.length)];
    operation2 = operations[random.nextInt(operations.length)];
    
    // ë‘ ìë¦¿ìˆ˜ ìƒì„±
    num1 = random.nextInt(90) + 10; // 10~99
    num2 = random.nextInt(90) + 10; // 10~99
    num3 = random.nextInt(90) + 10; // 10~99
    
    // ì¤‘ê°„ ê²°ê³¼ ê³„ì‚°
    int intermediateResult;
    if (operation == '+') {
      intermediateResult = num1! + num2!;
    } else {
      intermediateResult = num1! - num2!;
    }
    
    // ìµœì¢… ê²°ê³¼ ê³„ì‚°
    if (operation2 == '+') {
      correctAnswer = intermediateResult + num3!;
    } else {
      correctAnswer = intermediateResult - num3!;
      
      // ê²°ê³¼ê°€ ìŒìˆ˜ê°€ ë˜ì§€ ì•Šë„ë¡ ì¡°ì •
      if (correctAnswer! < 0) {
        final temp = num2;
        num2 = num3;
        num3 = temp;
        operation2 = '+';
        correctAnswer = intermediateResult + num3!;
      }
    }
  }

->

  void _generateThreeTermQuestion() {
    final random = Random();
    isThreeTermQuestion = true;
    
    // ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ì™€ ë‘ ë²ˆì§¸ ì—°ì‚° ì„ íƒ
    final operations = ['+', '-'];
    operation = operations[random.nextInt(operations.length)];
    operation2 = operations[random.nextInt(operations.length)];
    
    // í•œìë¦¿ìˆ˜ ìƒì„± (1~9)
    num1 = random.nextInt(9) + 1; // 1~9
    num2 = random.nextInt(9) + 1; // 1~9
    num3 = random.nextInt(9) + 1; // 1~9
    
    // ì¤‘ê°„ ê²°ê³¼ ê³„ì‚°
    int intermediateResult;
    if (operation == '+') {
      intermediateResult = num1! + num2!;
    } else {
      // ëº„ì…ˆì—ì„œ ìŒìˆ˜ê°€ ë‚˜ì˜¤ì§€ ì•Šë„ë¡ ë” í° ìˆ˜ì—ì„œ ì‘ì€ ìˆ˜ë¥¼ ë¹¼ë„ë¡ ì¡°ì •
      if (num1! < num2!) {
        final temp = num1;
        num1 = num2;
        num2 = temp;
      }
      intermediateResult = num1! - num2!;
    }
    
    // ìµœì¢… ê²°ê³¼ ê³„ì‚°
    if (operation2 == '+') {
      correctAnswer = intermediateResult + num3!;
    } else {
      // ëº„ì…ˆì¼ ë•Œ ìŒìˆ˜ê°€ ë‚˜ì˜¤ì§€ ì•Šë„ë¡ ì¡°ì •
      if (intermediateResult < num3!) {
        operation2 = '+';
        correctAnswer = intermediateResult + num3!;
      } else {
        correctAnswer = intermediateResult - num3!;
      }
    }
  }
```

```dart
    try {
      // ê¶Œí•œ ìš”ì²­
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        final permission = await Permission.storage.request();
        if (!permission.isGranted) {
```

```dart
  Future<void> saveImageToGallery(String imagePath) async {
    try {
      // ê¶Œí•œ ìš”ì²­
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        final permission = await Permission.storage.request();
        if (!permission.isGranted) {
          ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
            const SnackBar(content: Text('ì €ì¥ì†Œ ê¶Œí•œì´ í•„ìš”í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.')),
          );
          return;
        }
      }

      // ì´ë¯¸ì§€ë¥¼ ë°”ì´íŠ¸ë¡œ ì½ê¸°
      final byteData = await rootBundle.load(imagePath);
      final bytes = byteData.buffer.asUint8List();

      // ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥
      final result = await ImageGallerySaver.saveImage(
        bytes,
        name: getCharacterName(imagePath),
        quality: 100,
      );

      if (result['isSuccess'] == true) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ê°€ ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤! ğŸ“¸')),
        );
      } else {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ì— ì‹¤íŒ¨í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.')),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        SnackBar(content: Text('ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ë°œìƒí–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤: $e')),
      );
    }
  }

->


```

```dart
class CharacterInfo {
  final int id;
  final String koreanName;
  final String englishName;
  final String skill;
  final int combat;
  final int intelligence;
  final int cuteness;
  final int rarity;

  CharacterInfo({
    required this.id,
    required this.koreanName,
    required this.englishName,
    required this.skill,
    required this.combat,
    required this.intelligence,
    required this.cuteness,
    required this.rarity,
  });
}

  static CharacterInfo? getCharacterInfo(String koreanName) {
    return _characters[koreanName];

class RewardScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final int score;
  final VoidCallback? onRefundKey;
  
  const RewardScreen({Key? key, required this.score, this.onRefundKey}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  State<RewardScreen> createState() => _RewardScreenState();
}

class _RewardScreenState extends State<RewardScreen> {
  String selectedImage = '';
  bool hasEarnedCharacter = false;
  CharacterInfo? selectedCharacterInfo;

  final List<String> rewardImages = [

    'brainrot_image/í”„ë£°ë¦¬ í”„ë£°ë¼.webp',
    'brainrot_image/í”„ë¦¬ê³  ì¹´ë©œë¡œ.webp',

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    hasEarnedCharacter = widget.score >= 8;
    if (hasEarnedCharacter) {
      selectRandomImage();
      saveCharacterToCollection();
    } else {
      // 8ì  ë¯¸ë§Œì¼ ë•Œ ì—´ì‡  ë°˜í™˜
      widget.onRefundKey?.call();
    }
  }

  void selectRandomImage() {
    final random = Random();
    setState(() {
      selectedImage = rewardImages[random.nextInt(rewardImages.length)];
      String characterName = getCharacterName(selectedImage);
      selectedCharacterInfo = CharacterDatabase.getCharacterInfo(characterName);
    });
  }

  Future<void> saveCharacterToCollection() async {
    if (selectedImage.isNotEmpty) {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      List<String> collectedCharacters = prefs.getStringList('collected_characters') ?? [];
      
      if (!collectedCharacters.contains(selectedImage)) {
        collectedCharacters.add(selectedImage);
        await prefs.setStringList('collected_characters', collectedCharacters);
      }
    }
  }

  String getCharacterName(String imagePath) {
    return imagePath
        .split('/')
        .last
        .replaceAll('.webp', '')
        .replaceAll('brainrot_image/', '');
  }

  // ë³„ í‘œì‹œ ìœ„ì ¯
  Widget buildStarsWidget(int rating) {
    return Row(
      mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
      children: List.generate(5, (index) {
        return Icon(
          index < rating ? Icons.star : Icons.star_border,
          color: Colors.amber,
          size: 18,
        );
      }),
    );
  }

  // ... existing code ...
```

ì•±ì´ ì‹¤í–‰ë˜ë©´ ë‹¤ìŒê³¼ ê°™ì´ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸í•´ë³´ì‹œë©´ ë©ë‹ˆë‹¤:

```dart
class CharacterInfo {
  final int id;
  final String koreanName;
  final String englishName;
  final String skill;
  final int combat;
  final int intelligence;
  final int cuteness;
  final int rarity;

  CharacterInfo({
    required this.id,
    required this.koreanName,
    required this.englishName,
    required this.skill,
    required this.combat,
    required this.intelligence,
    required this.cuteness,
    required this.rarity,
  });
}

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    loadCollectedCharacters();
  }

  Future<void> loadCollectedCharacters() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    setState(() {
      collectedCharacters = prefs.getStringList('collected_characters') ?? [];
    });
  }

  String getCharacterName(String imagePath) {
    return imagePath
        .split('/')
        .last
        .replaceAll('.webp', '')
        .replaceAll('brainrot_image/', '');
  }

  // ë³„ í‘œì‹œ ìœ„ì ¯ (ì±„ì›Œì§„ ë³„ë§Œ í‘œì‹œ)
  Widget buildStarsWidget(int rating) {
    return Row(
      mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
      children: List.generate(rating, (index) {
        return const Icon(
          Icons.star,
          color: Colors.amber,
          size: 18,
        );
      }),
    );
  }
```

```dart

        keys++;
      });
      await prefs.setInt('keys', keys);
      print('Key refunded! Current keys: $keys'); // ë””ë²„ê·¸ìš©
```

```dart
  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    hasEarnedCharacter = widget.score >= 8;
    print('RewardScreen initState: score = ${widget.score}, hasEarnedCharacter = $hasEarnedCharacter');
    if (hasEarnedCharacter) {
      selectRandomImage();
      saveCharacterToCollection();
      // 8ì  ì´ìƒì¼ ë•Œë§Œ ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê°
```

```dart
      useKeyDirectly();

      print('8ì  ë¯¸ë§Œì´ë¼ ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê°í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ');
    }

  Future<void> useKeyDirectly() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      int keys = prefs.getInt('keys') ?? 5;
      print('í˜„ì¬ ì—´ì‡  ê°œìˆ˜: $keys');
      
      if (keys > 0) {
        keys--;
        await prefs.setInt('keys', keys);
        print('ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê° ì™„ë£Œ. ë‚¨ì€ ì—´ì‡ : $keys');
      } else {
        print('ì—´ì‡ ê°€ 0ê°œë¼ì„œ ì°¨ê°í•  ìˆ˜ ì—†ìŒ');
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê° ì¤‘ ì˜¤ë¥˜ ë°œìƒ: $e');
    }
  }
```

ë§ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤! Chrome ì›¹ì—ì„œëŠ” íƒ€ì´ë¨¸ê°€ ë‹¤ë¥´ê²Œ ë™ì‘í•  ìˆ˜ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ ë””ë²„ê¹…í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ë¨¼ì € ë¬´ì—‡ì´ ë¬¸ì œì¸ì§€ í™•ì¸í•˜ê¸° ìœ„í•´ ë””ë²„ê·¸ ë©”ì‹œì§€ë¥¼ ì¶”ê°€í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

```dart
  Future<void> _updateTimeUntilNextKey() async {
    if (keys >= 5) {
      setState(() {
        timeUntilNextKey = '';
      });
      return;
    }
    
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final lastKeyTime = prefs.getInt('last_key_time') ?? DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
    final now = DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
    const keyRechargeTime = 60 * 1000; // í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ìš©: 1ë¶„
    
    final nextKeyTime = lastKeyTime + keyRechargeTime;
    final timeLeft = nextKeyTime - now;
    
    if (timeLeft <= 0) {
      await checkKeyRecharge();
    } else {
      final hours = (timeLeft ~/ (1000 * 60 * 60));
      final minutes = ((timeLeft % (1000 * 60 * 60)) ~/ (1000 * 60));
      final seconds = ((timeLeft % (1000 * 60)) ~/ 1000);
      
      setState(() {
        timeUntilNextKey = '${hours.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}:${minutes.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}:${seconds.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}';
      });
    }
  }

->

  Future<void> _updateTimeUntilNextKey() async {
    if (keys >= 5) {
      setState(() {
        timeUntilNextKey = '';
      });
      return;
    }
    
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final lastKeyTime = prefs.getInt('last_key_time') ?? DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
    final now = DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
    const keyRechargeTime = 60 * 1000; // í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ìš©: 1ë¶„
    
    print('DEBUG: lastKeyTime = $lastKeyTime, now = $now, diff = ${now - lastKeyTime}ms');
    
    final nextKeyTime = lastKeyTime + keyRechargeTime;
    final timeLeft = nextKeyTime - now;
    
    print('DEBUG: timeLeft = ${timeLeft}ms');
    
    if (timeLeft <= 0) {
      print('DEBUG: ì‹œê°„ì´ ì§€ë‚˜ì„œ ì—´ì‡  ì¶©ì „ ì²´í¬');
      await checkKeyRecharge();
    } else {
      final hours = (timeLeft ~/ (1000 * 60 * 60));
      final minutes = ((timeLeft % (1000 * 60 * 60)) ~/ (1000 * 60));
      final seconds = ((timeLeft % (1000 * 60)) ~/ 1000);
      
      final timeString = '${hours.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}:${minutes.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}:${seconds.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}';
      print('DEBUG: ì¹´ìš´íŠ¸ë‹¤ìš´ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸: $timeString');
      
      setState(() {
        timeUntilNextKey = timeString;
      });
    }
  }
```

```dart
  // ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ ê¸°ëŠ¥
  Future<void> saveImageToGallery(String imagePath) async {
    try {
      // ê¶Œí•œ í™•ì¸
      var status = await Permission.storage.status;
      if (!status.isGranted) {
        await Permission.storage.request();
      }

      // Android 13+ ì—ì„œëŠ” photos ê¶Œí•œì´ í•„ìš”
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        var photoStatus = await Permission.photos.status;
        if (!photoStatus.isGranted) {
          await Permission.photos.request();
        }
      }

      // assetsì—ì„œ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì½ê¸°
      final byteData = await rootBundle.load(imagePath);
      final bytes = byteData.buffer.asUint8List();
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
      final tempDir = await getTemporaryDirectory();
      final fileName = imagePath.split('/').last;
      final tempFile = File('${tempDir.path}/$fileName');
      await tempFile.writeAsBytes(bytes);
      
      // ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥
      await Gal.putImage(tempFile.path, album: 'ë¸Œë ˆì¸ë¡¯ ìˆ˜í•™ê²Œì„');
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ì‚­ì œ
      await tempFile.delete();
      
      // ì„±ê³µ ë©”ì‹œì§€
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ê°€ ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤!'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.green,
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨: $e');
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ì— ì‹¤íŒ¨í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

  Widget _buildDefaultRewardImage() {
    return Container(
      width: 300,
      height: 300,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.grey[300],
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(15),
      ),
      child: Column(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
        children: [
          Icon(
            Icons.emoji_events,
            size: 80,
            color: Colors.amber[600],
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 10),
          Text(
            'ì¶•í•˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤!',
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 18,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              color: Colors.grey[700],
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
```

```dart

import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';
```

```dart
import 'dart:typed_data';

// ... existing code ...

class _CollectionScreenState extends State<CollectionScreen> {
  List<String> collectedCharacters = [];
  
  // ... existing code ...

  String getCharacterName(String imagePath) {
    return imagePath
        .split('/')
        .last
        .replaceAll('.webp', '')
        .replaceAll('brainrot_image/', '');
  }

  // ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ ê¸°ëŠ¥
  Future<void> saveImageToGallery(String imagePath) async {
    try {
      // ê¶Œí•œ í™•ì¸
      var status = await Permission.storage.status;
      if (!status.isGranted) {
        await Permission.storage.request();
      }

      // Android 13+ ì—ì„œëŠ” photos ê¶Œí•œì´ í•„ìš”
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        var photoStatus = await Permission.photos.status;
        if (!photoStatus.isGranted) {
          await Permission.photos.request();
        }
      }

      // assetsì—ì„œ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì½ê¸°
      final byteData = await rootBundle.load(imagePath);
      final bytes = byteData.buffer.asUint8List();
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
      final tempDir = await getTemporaryDirectory();
      final fileName = imagePath.split('/').last;
      final tempFile = File('${tempDir.path}/$fileName');
      await tempFile.writeAsBytes(bytes);
      
      // ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥
      await Gal.putImage(tempFile.path, album: 'ë¸Œë ˆì¸ë¡¯ ìˆ˜í•™ê²Œì„');
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ì‚­ì œ
      await tempFile.delete();
      
      // ì„±ê³µ ë©”ì‹œì§€
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ê°€ ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤!'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.green,
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨: $e');
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ì— ì‹¤íŒ¨í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

  // ... existing code ...
```

```dart
  // ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ ê¸°ëŠ¥
  Future<void> saveImageToGallery(String imagePath) async {
    try {
      // ê¶Œí•œ í™•ì¸
      var status = await Permission.storage.status;
      if (!status.isGranted) {
        await Permission.storage.request();
      }

      // Android 13+ ì—ì„œëŠ” photos ê¶Œí•œì´ í•„ìš”
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        var photoStatus = await Permission.photos.status;
        if (!photoStatus.isGranted) {
          await Permission.photos.request();
        }
      }

      // assetsì—ì„œ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì½ê¸°
      final byteData = await rootBundle.load(imagePath);
      final bytes = byteData.buffer.asUint8List();
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
      final tempDir = await getTemporaryDirectory();
      final fileName = imagePath.split('/').last;
      final tempFile = File('${tempDir.path}/$fileName');
      await tempFile.writeAsBytes(bytes);
      
      // ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥
      await Gal.putImage(tempFile.path, album: 'ë¸Œë ˆì¸ë¡¯ ìˆ˜í•™ê²Œì„');
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ì‚­ì œ
      await tempFile.delete();
      
      // ì„±ê³µ ë©”ì‹œì§€
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ê°€ ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤!'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.green,
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨: $e');
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ì— ì‹¤íŒ¨í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

->

  // ìºë¦­í„° ì •ë³´ ìº¡ì³ ë° ì €ì¥ ê¸°ëŠ¥
  Future<void> captureAndSaveCharacterInfo() async {
    try {
      // ê¶Œí•œ í™•ì¸
      var status = await Permission.storage.status;
      if (!status.isGranted) {
        await Permission.storage.request();
      }

      // Android 13+ ì—ì„œëŠ” photos ê¶Œí•œì´ í•„ìš”
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        var photoStatus = await Permission.photos.status;
        if (!photoStatus.isGranted) {
          await Permission.photos.request();
        }
      }

      // RepaintBoundaryë¡œ ê°ì‹¸ì§„ ìœ„ì ¯ ìº¡ì³
      RenderRepaintBoundary boundary = _repaintBoundaryKey.currentContext!
          .findRenderObject() as RenderRepaintBoundary;
      
      // ì´ë¯¸ì§€ë¡œ ë³€í™˜ (ê³ í•´ìƒë„)
      ui.Image image = await boundary.toImage(pixelRatio: 3.0);
      
      // PNG í˜•ì‹ìœ¼ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
      ByteData? byteData = await image.toByteData(format: ui.ImageByteFormat.png);
      Uint8List pngBytes = byteData!.buffer.asUint8List();
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
      final tempDir = await getTemporaryDirectory();
      final characterName = getCharacterName(selectedImage);
      final fileName = '${characterName}_ì •ë³´.png';
      final tempFile = File('${tempDir.path}/$fileName');
      await tempFile.writeAsBytes(pngBytes);
      
      // ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥
      await Gal.putImage(tempFile.path, album: 'ë¸Œë ˆì¸ë¡¯ ìˆ˜í•™ê²Œì„');
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ì‚­ì œ
      await tempFile.delete();
      
      // ì„±ê³µ ë©”ì‹œì§€
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ìºë¦­í„° ì •ë³´ê°€ ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤!'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.green,
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('ìºë¦­í„° ì •ë³´ ìº¡ì³ ì‹¤íŒ¨: $e');
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ìºë¦­í„° ì •ë³´ ì €ì¥ì— ì‹¤íŒ¨í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }
```

ì´ì œ ìºë¦­í„° ì •ë³´ë¥¼ ë‹´ê³  ìˆëŠ” ìœ„ì ¯ì„ RepaintBoundaryë¡œ ê°ì‹¸ê³ , ì €ì¥ ë²„íŠ¼ì„ ìˆ˜ì •í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.


ì´ì œ ë„ê° í™”ë©´ë„ ê°™ì€ ë°©ì‹ìœ¼ë¡œ ìˆ˜ì •í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';
import 'package:gal/gal.dart';
import 'package:permission_handler/permission_handler.dart';
import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';
import 'dart:io';
import 'dart:typed_data';
import 'dart:ui' as ui;
import 'package:flutter/rendering.dart';
```

```dart
  // ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ ê¸°ëŠ¥
  Future<void> saveImageToGallery(String imagePath) async {
    try {
      // ê¶Œí•œ í™•ì¸
      var status = await Permission.storage.status;
      if (!status.isGranted) {
        await Permission.storage.request();
      }

      // Android 13+ ì—ì„œëŠ” photos ê¶Œí•œì´ í•„ìš”
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        var photoStatus = await Permission.photos.status;
        if (!photoStatus.isGranted) {
          await Permission.photos.request();
        }
      }

      // assetsì—ì„œ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì½ê¸°
      final byteData = await rootBundle.load(imagePath);
      final bytes = byteData.buffer.asUint8List();
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
      final tempDir = await getTemporaryDirectory();
      final fileName = imagePath.split('/').last;
      final tempFile = File('${tempDir.path}/$fileName');
      await tempFile.writeAsBytes(bytes);
      
      // ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥
      await Gal.putImage(tempFile.path, album: 'ë¸Œë ˆì¸ë¡¯ ìˆ˜í•™ê²Œì„');
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ì‚­ì œ
      await tempFile.delete();
      
      // ì„±ê³µ ë©”ì‹œì§€
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ê°€ ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤!'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.green,
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨: $e');
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì €ì¥ì— ì‹¤íŒ¨í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

->

  // ìºë¦­í„° ì •ë³´ ìº¡ì³ ë° ì €ì¥ ê¸°ëŠ¥
  Future<void> captureAndSaveCharacterInfo(GlobalKey repaintBoundaryKey, String characterName) async {
    try {
      // ê¶Œí•œ í™•ì¸
      var status = await Permission.storage.status;
      if (!status.isGranted) {
        await Permission.storage.request();
      }

      // Android 13+ ì—ì„œëŠ” photos ê¶Œí•œì´ í•„ìš”
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        var photoStatus = await Permission.photos.status;
        if (!photoStatus.isGranted) {
          await Permission.photos.request();
        }
      }

      // RepaintBoundaryë¡œ ê°ì‹¸ì§„ ìœ„ì ¯ ìº¡ì³
      RenderRepaintBoundary boundary = repaintBoundaryKey.currentContext!
          .findRenderObject() as RenderRepaintBoundary;
      
      // ì´ë¯¸ì§€ë¡œ ë³€í™˜ (ê³ í•´ìƒë„)
      ui.Image image = await boundary.toImage(pixelRatio: 3.0);
      
      // PNG í˜•ì‹ìœ¼ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
      ByteData? byteData = await image.toByteData(format: ui.ImageByteFormat.png);
      Uint8List pngBytes = byteData!.buffer.asUint8List();
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
      final tempDir = await getTemporaryDirectory();
      final fileName = '${characterName}_ì •ë³´.png';
      final tempFile = File('${tempDir.path}/$fileName');
      await tempFile.writeAsBytes(pngBytes);
      
      // ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥
      await Gal.putImage(tempFile.path, album: 'ë¸Œë ˆì¸ë¡¯ ìˆ˜í•™ê²Œì„');
      
      // ì„ì‹œ íŒŒì¼ ì‚­ì œ
      await tempFile.delete();
      
      // ì„±ê³µ ë©”ì‹œì§€
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ìºë¦­í„° ì •ë³´ê°€ ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ì— ì €ì¥ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤!'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.green,
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('ìºë¦­í„° ì •ë³´ ìº¡ì³ ì‹¤íŒ¨: $e');
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('ìºë¦­í„° ì •ë³´ ì €ì¥ì— ì‹¤íŒ¨í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }
```

```dart
void selectRandomImage() {
  final random = Random();
  setState(() {
    selectedImage = rewardImages[random.nextInt(rewardImages.length)];
    // ì „ì²´ 41ê°œ ìºë¦­í„° ì¤‘ì—ì„œ ì™„ì „ ë¬´ì‘ìœ„ ì„ íƒ

  // ì´ë¯¸ ê°€ì§„ ìºë¦­í„°ì¸ì§€ í™•ì¸

    collectedCharacters.add(selectedImage); // ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ì¶”ê°€
```

```dart
  void selectRandomImage() {
    final random = Random();
    setState(() {
      selectedImage = rewardImages[random.nextInt(rewardImages.length)];
      String characterName = getCharacterName(selectedImage);
      selectedCharacterInfo = CharacterDatabase.getCharacterInfo(characterName);
    });
  }

->

  Future<void> selectRandomImage() async {
    final random = Random();
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    List<String> collectedCharacters = prefs.getStringList('collected_characters') ?? [];
    
    // ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ëª©ë¡ ê³„ì‚°
    List<String> uncollectedCharacters = rewardImages
        .where((character) => !collectedCharacters.contains(character))
        .toList();
    
    setState(() {
      if (uncollectedCharacters.isNotEmpty) {
        // ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ: ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ì¤‘ì—ì„œë§Œ ì„ íƒ
        selectedImage = uncollectedCharacters[random.nextInt(uncollectedCharacters.length)];
        print('ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ: ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ${uncollectedCharacters.length}ê°œ ì¤‘ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ');
      } else {
        // ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ: ë„ê° 100% ë‹¬ì„± ì‹œ ì „ì²´ ìºë¦­í„°ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ
        selectedImage = rewardImages[random.nextInt(rewardImages.length)];
        print('ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ: ë„ê° 100% ë‹¬ì„±ìœ¼ë¡œ ì „ì²´ ìºë¦­í„°ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ');
      }
      
      String characterName = getCharacterName(selectedImage);
      selectedCharacterInfo = CharacterDatabase.getCharacterInfo(characterName);
      print('ì„ íƒëœ ìºë¦­í„°: $characterName');
    });
  }
```

ì´ì œ initStateì—ì„œ selectRandomImageë¥¼ í˜¸ì¶œí•˜ëŠ” ë¶€ë¶„ë„ ìˆ˜ì •í•´ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

```dart

  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    hasEarnedCharacter = widget.score >= 8;
    print('RewardScreen initState: score = ${widget.score}, hasEarnedCharacter = $hasEarnedCharacter');
    if (hasEarnedCharacter) {
      selectRandomImage();
      saveCharacterToCollection();
      // 8ì  ì´ìƒì¼ ë•Œë§Œ ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê°
      print('ì§ì ‘ ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê° ì‹œë„...');
      useKeyDirectly();
    } else {
      print('8ì  ë¯¸ë§Œì´ë¼ ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê°í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ');
    }
  }

->

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    hasEarnedCharacter = widget.score >= 8;
    print('RewardScreen initState: score = ${widget.score}, hasEarnedCharacter = $hasEarnedCharacter');
    if (hasEarnedCharacter) {
      _initializeReward();
    } else {
      print('8ì  ë¯¸ë§Œì´ë¼ ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê°í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ');
    }
  }

  Future<void> _initializeReward() async {
    await selectRandomImage();
    await saveCharacterToCollection();
    // 8ì  ì´ìƒì¼ ë•Œë§Œ ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê°
    print('ì§ì ‘ ì—´ì‡  ì°¨ê° ì‹œë„...');
    useKeyDirectly();
  }
```

```dart
class _RewardScreenState extends State<RewardScreen> {
  String selectedImage = '';
  bool hasEarnedCharacter = false;
  CharacterInfo? selectedCharacterInfo;
  final GlobalKey _repaintBoundaryKey = GlobalKey();
  bool isAllCollected = false;
  int totalCharacters = 41;
  int collectedCount = 0;
```

```dart
  Future<void> selectRandomImage() async {
    final random = Random();
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    List<String> collectedCharacters = prefs.getStringList('collected_characters') ?? [];
    
    // ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ëª©ë¡ ê³„ì‚°
    List<String> uncollectedCharacters = rewardImages
        .where((character) => !collectedCharacters.contains(character))
        .toList();
    
    setState(() {
      if (uncollectedCharacters.isNotEmpty) {
        // ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ: ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ì¤‘ì—ì„œë§Œ ì„ íƒ
        selectedImage = uncollectedCharacters[random.nextInt(uncollectedCharacters.length)];
        print('ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ: ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ${uncollectedCharacters.length}ê°œ ì¤‘ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ');
      } else {
        // ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ: ë„ê° 100% ë‹¬ì„± ì‹œ ì „ì²´ ìºë¦­í„°ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ
        selectedImage = rewardImages[random.nextInt(rewardImages.length)];
        print('ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ: ë„ê° 100% ë‹¬ì„±ìœ¼ë¡œ ì „ì²´ ìºë¦­í„°ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ');
      }
      
      String characterName = getCharacterName(selectedImage);
      selectedCharacterInfo = CharacterDatabase.getCharacterInfo(characterName);
      print('ì„ íƒëœ ìºë¦­í„°: $characterName');
    });
  }

->

  Future<void> selectRandomImage() async {
    final random = Random();
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    List<String> collectedCharacters = prefs.getStringList('collected_characters') ?? [];
    
    // ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ëª©ë¡ ê³„ì‚°
    List<String> uncollectedCharacters = rewardImages
        .where((character) => !collectedCharacters.contains(character))
        .toList();
    
    setState(() {
      collectedCount = collectedCharacters.length;
      isAllCollected = uncollectedCharacters.isEmpty;
      
      if (uncollectedCharacters.isNotEmpty) {
        // ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ: ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ì¤‘ì—ì„œë§Œ ì„ íƒ
        selectedImage = uncollectedCharacters[random.nextInt(uncollectedCharacters.length)];
        print('ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ: ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ${uncollectedCharacters.length}ê°œ ì¤‘ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ');
      } else {
        // ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ: ë„ê° 100% ë‹¬ì„± ì‹œ ì „ì²´ ìºë¦­í„°ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ
        selectedImage = rewardImages[random.nextInt(rewardImages.length)];
        print('ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ: ë„ê° 100% ë‹¬ì„±ìœ¼ë¡œ ì „ì²´ ìºë¦­í„°ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ');
      }
      
      String characterName = getCharacterName(selectedImage);
      selectedCharacterInfo = CharacterDatabase.getCharacterInfo(characterName);
      print('ì„ íƒëœ ìºë¦­í„°: $characterName');
    });
  }
```

## ğŸ”„ ìŠ¤ë§ˆíŠ¸ ì¶”ì¶œ ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ

### 1. **ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ** (ê¸°ë³¸)

- ì¤‘ë³µ ì—†ëŠ” íš¨ìœ¨ì ì¸ ìˆ˜ì§‘ ê²½í—˜
- ì½˜ì†” ë¡œê·¸: `"ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ: ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° Xê°œ ì¤‘ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ"`

### 2. **ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ** (100% ë‹¬ì„± ì‹œ)
- ë„ê° 100% ì™„ì„± ì‹œ **ì „ì²´ ìºë¦­í„°**ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ
- ì™„ì„± í›„ì—ë„ ê²Œì„ì„ ì¦ê¸¸ ìˆ˜ ìˆìŒ
- ì½˜ì†” ë¡œê·¸: `"ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ: ë„ê° 100% ë‹¬ì„±ìœ¼ë¡œ ì „ì²´ ìºë¦­í„°ì—ì„œ ì„ íƒ"`

- ìƒˆë¡œìš´ ìºë¦­í„°ê°€ ì¶”ê°€ë˜ë©´ **ìë™ìœ¼ë¡œ ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ**ë¡œ ë³µê·€
- ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ ì‹œì—ë„ íš¨ìœ¨ì ì¸ ìˆ˜ì§‘ ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ìœ ì§€

## ğŸ“Š UI ê°œì„ ì‚¬í•­

### ğŸ¨ ìˆ˜ì§‘ ì§„í–‰ ìƒí™© í‘œì‹œ
```

ğŸ‰ ë„ê° ì™„ì„±! (ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ)           // ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“œ
```

### ğŸ¯ ëª¨ë“œë³„ UI ìƒ‰ìƒ
- **ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ**: íŒŒë€ìƒ‰ ë°°ì§€ (ì§„í–‰ ì¤‘)
- **ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ**: ì´ˆë¡ìƒ‰ ë°°ì§€ (ì™„ì„±)

## ğŸ”§ ê¸°ìˆ ì  êµ¬í˜„

### í•µì‹¬ ë¡œì§:
```dart
// ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„° ê³„ì‚°
List<String> uncollectedCharacters = rewardImages
    .where((character) => !collectedCharacters.contains(character))
    .toList();

if (uncollectedCharacters.isNotEmpty) {
    // ë¹„ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ: ë¯¸ìˆ˜ì§‘ ìºë¦­í„°ë§Œ
    selectedImage = uncollectedCharacters[random.nextInt(uncollectedCharacters.length)];
} else {
    // ë³µì›ì¶”ì¶œ: ì „ì²´ ìºë¦­í„°
    selectedImage = rewardImages[random.nextInt(rewardImages.length)];
}
```

### ğŸ¯ ì‚¬ìš©ì ê²½í—˜ ê°œì„ :
